HLP
NP25 *** Flashpro Command HELP ***

 TYP  Set parameter for write
 LOD  Download HEX file
 BLN  ROM Blank check
 PRG  ROM Program
 ERS  ROM all Erase
 VRF  ROM Verify
 EPV  ROM Erase & Program & Verify
 HEX  Dump HEX file
 SIG  Display Silicon Signature
 STS  Display setting parameter
 SPY  Target Supply status
 RES  Flashpro RESET
 PLD  PROM Load
 OPT  Flashpro option command
 VER  FP3 firmware version
 BRT  Host UART speed set
 VOL  Voltage set

 TYP  Set parameter for write
 LOD  Download HEX file
 BLN  ROM Blank check
